## SAP S/4HANA® Financial Accounting Certification Guide  
### Application Associate Exam  

Dear Reader,  

Close your eyes and imagine it: The audience cheers, you take a bow, and the curtains close. You’ve sunk your heart and soul into your performance, and you can breathe a sigh of joyful relief knowing you’ve played your absolute best. All those hours of **dedication** have finally paid off!  

But before you can reach this happy point, you need to put in the **work**. Only with regular **practice** can you gain the **confidence** you’ll need to succeed, whether you’re about to perform a recital or sit for the **SAP S/4HANA financial accounting associate exam**.  

Author **Stefanos Pougkas** returns with a **third edition** of this certification guide filled with **practice questions** to help you fine-tune your **financial accounting skills**. And Stefanos isn’t just a review coach — he wrote the exam itself, too! With **real-world examples** and **insider tips**, this guide is the warmup you need to **ace the test** and take that congratulatory bow.

## 15 Preface

The **SAP PRESS Certification Guide Series** is designed to provide those preparing to take an **SAP-certified exam** with all the review, insight, and practice needed to pass the exam. The series is written in **practical, easy-to-follow language** focused on what is necessary to successfully pass your exam.

### Target Audience

This book is written specifically for those preparing to take the **SAP Certified Application Associate – SAP S/4HANA for Financial Accounting Associates C_TS4FI_2020 exam**. It focuses on core **SAP S/4HANA financial accounting skills**: general ledger accounting, accounts payable and accounts receivable, asset accounting, financial closing, and more.

By using this book, you will gain a thorough understanding of the **exam structure** and what to expect when taking it. It offers a refresher on **key concepts** covered in the exam and the opportunity to test your skills with **sample practice questions and answers**.

This book aligns closely with the **course syllabus** and the exam structure, ensuring all information is relevant and applicable. The features and SAP products are explained using practical examples and straightforward language so you can prepare for the exam and improve daily work skills.

Each book in this series is structured to highlight exactly what you need to know.

---

## Structure of This Book

Each chapter begins with a clear list of **learning objectives**; for example:

### Techniques You’ll Master

- Prepare for the exam  
- Understand the general exam structure  
- Answer practice questions  

From here, you will dive into the chapter and get right into the **test objective coverage**. Throughout the book, several helpful elements are provided:

- **Tips**: Call out useful information about related ideas and practical suggestions for using functions.  
- **Notes**: Provide other resources or special SAP tools and services relevant to the topic.  
- **Warnings**: Highlight points that often cause confusion or are commonly overlooked.

---

### Example Elements

**Tip:**  
This book contains screenshots and diagrams to improve your understanding of many information modeling concepts.

**Note:**  
This certification guide covers all topics you need to successfully pass the exam and provides sample questions similar to those found on the actual exam.

**Warning:**  
This book is meant to review and supplement knowledge gained from standard **SAP Training and Adoption training**.

---

### Typical Chapter Structure

- **Introductory bullets:** Discuss the techniques you must master to be proficient in the topic.  
- **Topic introduction:** Provides a general overview and objectives for the exam topic.  
- **Real-world scenario:** Presents a scenario showing how these skills apply in practical situations.  
- **Objectives:** Necessary information to successfully pass the test portion.

---

### Important Terminology

Just before practice questions, there is a section to review **important terminology** with definitions drawn from the chapter.

### Practice Questions

The chapter provides a series of **practice questions** related to the topic. The question formats mimic those found on the certification exam.

### Practice Question Answers and Explanations

After questions, answers are provided with explanations detailing why answers are correct or incorrect.

### Test Takeaway

This section reviews the key areas you should now understand.

### Summary

Concludes the chapter with a summary of topics covered.

---

## Overview of Chapters

- **Chapter 1: Overview and Deployment of SAP S/4HANA**  
  Focus on the architecture of **SAP HANA**, deployment options of **SAP S/4HANA**, and basic functions of the **SAP Fiori user interface**.

- **Chapter 2: General Ledger Accounting**  
  Covers general ledger accounting in SAP S/4HANA, including configuration of financial organizational units, chart of accounts design, general ledger master records, and document posting controls.

- **Chapter 3: Accounts Payable and Accounts Receivable**  
  Explores accounts payable and receivable processes, business partner master record maintenance, invoicing, payments, dunning, and correspondence.

- **Chapter 4: Asset Accounting**  
  Discusses asset accounting organizational units such as chart of depreciation and asset classes, integration with general ledger, asset accounting transactions, and period-end closing.

- **Chapter 5: Financial Closing**  
  Details month-end and year-end closing processes including balance confirmations, accrual management, foreign currency valuation, bad debt reserves, open item reclassification, and the **SAP S/4HANA Financial Closing cockpit**.

- **Chapter 6: Organizational Assignments and Process Integration**  
  Focuses on key functionalities of SAP financials, including using special general ledger indicators, document parking, and creating posting validations and substitutions.

---

## Practice Questions Overview

Before starting practice questions, here’s some background on their structure:

- **Question:** Read carefully as wording impacts the answer.  
- **Question Hint:** Indicates how many answers are correct (single or multiple).  
- **Answers:** Vary based on question type:

  - Multiple response: More than one correct answer possible.  
  - Multiple choice: Only one correct answer.  
  - True/false: One correct answer (used only in this book to test understanding, not in the exam).  

---

## Summary

This certification guide helps you approach content and key concepts for each exam topic. Through practice questions and detailed explanations, you gain insights into question types, formulations, and answers.

Understanding the relationship between questions and answers is as vital as understanding the content. This book equips you with the knowledge and tools needed to become a **SAP Certified Application Associate in SAP S/4HANA for financial accounting**.

---

## Introduction: The Path to Certification

### Techniques You’ll Master

- Understand the relevant **certification offerings** for finance in SAP S/4HANA  
- Find the **courses required** for certification  
- Learn **techniques for taking certification exams**  
- Identify further relevant **SAP Training and Adoption offerings** in SAP S/4HANA  
- Explore additional **resources for financials** in SAP S/4HANA  
- Expand your knowledge and **keep skills up to date**  

---

This chapter provides an overview of the **SAP S/4HANA for Financial Accounting Associates exam and certification**. It covers levels and offerings for **SAP financial certifications**, identifies study resources, and provides **test-taking advice**.

With SAP S/4HANA, SAP introduces a new class of **enterprise resource planning (ERP)** solutions designed to keep businesses competitive and support digital transformation.

**SAP S/4HANA** is the most important product in the SAP portfolio, with **financial accounting** at the core of its processes and functionalities. As adoption grows worldwide, the demand increases for **implementation and support consultants** skilled in core financial functions.

This chapter aims to establish why the **SAP S/4HANA for Financial Accounting Associates certification** is ideal for you. It details the certification, essential **SAP Training and Adoption materials**, ways to access these materials, and tips to prepare and succeed in the exam.

## Additional Resources for SAP S/4HANA Exam Preparation

Finally, we’ll look at some additional resources you might find useful when preparing for the **SAP S/4HANA** exam and as you continue your journey with **SAP S/4HANA**.

---

## Who This Book Is For

You’ll be hard-pressed to find any **SAP project worldwide** that doesn’t require project members familiar with **financial accounting processes** and configuration. This was true for **SAP ERP** and remains true for **SAP S/4HANA**. This makes **financial accounting consultants** with good skills and solid experience a valuable and sought-after resource for both **SAP partner firms** and **SAP customers**.

This book covers a broad and deep scope of core financial accounting configuration and business processes in the **SAP S/4HANA system**. As such, it is an excellent starting point for those just getting introduced to **financial accounting**. For example, you might be:

- A new hire at an **SAP implementation partner**
- An IT support consultant whose company is upgrading to **SAP S/4HANA**
- A graduate looking to kick-start a career in **SAP**

The book is also a great way for more experienced consultants to revisit the basics. Often, as you gain experience, you specialize in a specific part of the **SAP financials world**. This book helps you look again at the complete picture of **financial accounting** and upskill on the specifics of **SAP S/4HANA**.

Those working as business users with **financial accounting** in SAP often want to expand beyond that role to gain a deeper and broader understanding of the implementation or to support consultant roles. Developers aiming to specialize in financials or gain a good understanding of common business processes configured in **SAP S/4HANA** can find value in this book, even just as a reference if they aren’t interested in the certification aspect.

The book is designed around the latest **2020 version** of the **SAP S/4HANA system** and certification; however, because it covers core processes that are mature, the knowledge should support future versions of the product as well.

---

## Certifications for SAP Financials in SAP S/4HANA

We’ll first review the portfolio of certifications from **SAP** that might be of interest, then go into the details of the **C_TS4FI_2020 certification**.

### Useful SAP S/4HANA Certifications Overview

**SAP** offers an expanding portfolio of certifications for **SAP S/4HANA**, many of which are relevant for the **financial accounting consultant**. Below is a list of potentially relevant certifications:

- **C_TS410_1909: SAP Certified Application Associate – Integrated Business Processes in SAP S/4HANA**  
  This certification validates a solid understanding of **integrated processes** in **SAP S/4HANA**, including basics, financial and management accounting, human capital management, enterprise asset management, lead to cash, design-to-operate processing, source-to-pay, project system, and warehouse management. It provides an immensely useful understanding of the nearly end-to-end scope of the SAP S/4HANA solution.

- **C_ACTIVATE12: SAP Certified Associate – SAP Activate Project Manager**  
  **SAP Activate** is the implementation methodology replacing **ASAP**. Based on **Agile**, it departs significantly from the traditional waterfall approach. All **SAP S/4HANA** projects use some form of **SAP Activate**. Understanding the methodology, accelerators, and implementation options benefits all consultants, not just project managers.

- **C_TS4CO_2020: SAP Certified Application Associate – Management Accounting with SAP S/4HANA**  
  This certification corresponds to the focus on **management accounting**. It’s useful for financial accounting consultants who want broader roles, as **financial accounting** and **controlling** are increasingly integrated. A [management accounting certification guide](https://www.sap-press.com/4886) by **SAP PRESS** is available and relevant.

- **C_TS4FI_2020: SAP Certified Application Associate – SAP S/4HANA for Financial Accounting Associates (SAP S/4HANA 1610)**  
  The certification for which this book is created, it’s the best starting point for new financial accounting consultants.

- **P_S4FIN_2020: SAP Certified Application Professional – Financials in SAP S/4HANA for SAP ERP Finance Experts**  
  The advanced certification for professionals with solid knowledge in both **financial accounting** and **controlling** who have upskilled to **SAP S/4HANA**. It’s the only professional-level certification for **financial accounting** with **SAP S/4HANA**.

- **C_S4CFI: SAP Certified Application Associate – SAP S/4HANA Cloud – Finance Implementation**  
  Essential for consultants in **SAP S/4HANA Cloud** implementations as finance experts. Covers detailed knowledge in financial accounting, management accounting, treasury, group reporting, innovation applications, and more. Requires maintaining certification through quarterly “stay-current” assessments via an **SAP Learning Hub** subscription.

- **C_S4FTR_2020: SAP Certified Application Associate – Treasury with SAP S/4HANA**  
  For consultants covering **treasury and risk management**, cash management, bank account management, cash operations, and liquidity management. Increasing adoption makes this worthwhile.

- **C_S4FCF_2020: SAP Certified Application Associate – Central Finance in SAP S/4HANA**  
  Focuses on the **Central Finance** deployment option, requiring both high technical knowledge and a broad understanding of finance functions.

---

### Exam Format for Certifications

Most certifications, including those mentioned and most in **SAP Training and Adoption**, follow the same format:

- **Length of exam:** Up to three hours
- **Number of questions:** 80, including multiple-choice or multiple-selection
- **Exam location:** Online via **SAP Certification Hub**, a subscription-based cloud service  
  - Annual subscription allows six certification attempts  
  - Three attempts allowed per individual certification  
  - Can take previous or next version of the certification depending on availability

You can also take exams at authorized certification centers in person. Visit [SAP Training and Adoption](https://training.sap.com/) or contact your local training office for more information.

---

### SAP Training and Adoption Learning Journeys

The **SAP Training and Adoption Web Shop** categorizes education content into **Learning Journeys**, which are interactive maps guiding you through complex training offerings. This can help you navigate the broad range of available **SAP training resources**.

---

## C_TS4FI_2020 Certification

The **C_TS4FI_2020** certification for **SAP S/4HANA** corresponds to the old **C_TFIN52** certification from **SAP ERP**, representing the common starting point for many **SAP financial accounting professionals**.

- Both the new certification and underlying course materials are based on **SAP ERP** content, so prior **SAP ERP** certification holders can easily identify differences and prepare to pass the **SAP S/4HANA** exam.
- The certification will likely continue an **annual release cycle** to match SAP S/4HANA release updates.
- Core **Customizing** and functionality coverage ensures the certification remains valid beyond the day it’s earned.
- The book remains a valuable reference for current and future certification releases.

---

### Certification Exam Format

The **C_TS4FI_2020** exam consists of:

- **80 questions**, including:
  - **Multiple-choice**: select 1 correct answer from 4 options
  - **Multiple-selection (type 1)**: select 2 correct answers from 4 options
  - **Multiple-selection (type 2)**: select 3 correct answers from 5 options  
- You must answer all parts correctly to get credit for the question.
- Passing requires **59% correct answers**, meaning at least **48 out of 80** questions correct.  
  - For version 1909, the 57% pass rate requires **46 correct answers**.  
- Pass rate may vary depending on question difficulty.

You can take the exam at a certified center or via the **cloud offering** at home. Check the [SAP Training and Adoption Shop](https://training.sap.com/shop/certification) or local training offices for details.

## Scope of the Certification Exam

The book is modeled closely on the **topic areas of the certification** (see Figure 4). There is some small variation: 

- **Special general ledger transactions** are included in the **accounts payable/accounts receivable** topics.
- **Bank account management** is included as a separate area in **organizational assignments and process integration**.

However, the book covers the same areas and scope as the exam itself and the academy courses on which the certification is based.

- The next version will refer to **SAP S/4HANA 2021**, scheduled for release in September 2021, with certification likely available early 2022.

### Tip

**Collections** are semi-arbitrary course version numbers that map a course to a specific product release. The higher the collection number, the newer the course. Always use the newest collection of materials available.

## Ways to Learn

You can choose to learn and consume the standard **SAP Training and Adoption courses** in a variety of ways:

### Classroom Training

- Offers **immediate live feedback** from expert trainers.
- Networking opportunities with peers.
- Minimal work interruptions during the day.
- System access to perform all exercises during training.
- Printed materials averaging more than 400 pages per course or week.

### Remote (Live) Classroom (SAP Live Class)

- Internet-based training that approximates classroom experience.
- Live trainer, system access, and peer interaction.
- Some differences compared to face-to-face classroom experience.
- Frequently used during the COVID-19 pandemic.

### SAP Learning Hub

A **cloud-based offering** with an annual subscription available at [SAP Training Shop](https://training.sap.com/shop/learninghub).

Includes:

- Access to SAP Training and Adoption catalog content, including **SAP S/4HANA** content available upon release.  
  - Delivered as either **e-books** (PDF) or **e-learning** (multimedia and simulations).  
  - **Figure 6** shows course search example for financial accounting in SAP S/4HANA.

- Access to **SAP Learning Rooms** for various lines of business, including Financial Accounting (Figure 7).  
  - Virtual forums for discussion, questions, webinars, and updates.  
  - Lead trainers facilitate and manage these rooms.

- **SAP Live Access** gives access to training systems configured for SAP Learning Hub courses.  
  - Subscription plus a **voucher** is needed for 20 or 60 hours of system access.  
  - You can suspend and resume activity or switch courses within allotted time.  
  - Planned support for all current and future financial courses in SAP S/4HANA.  
  - **Figure 8** shows SAP Live Access portal and course catalog.

## Advice for Taking the Certification Exam

Studying the education materials is the key to passing the certification. Besides that, understanding the question types is important.

---

### Realign Your Perspective

This book aims to help you pass the certification exam **C_TS4FI_2020: SAP Certified Application Associate – SAP S/4HANA for Financial Accounting Associates (SAP S/4HANA 2020)**.

- **Certification focus**: Knowledge of specific course materials.
- **Consulting projects**: Broader experience and problem solving.
- **Certification exam** is not about best practices but about the **only practice** as defined by exam content.

Experience supports success but **knowledge and understanding of the training materials** is essential for passing the exam.

---

### What to Expect When Taking the Exam

- The exam consists of **multiple-choice** and **multiple-selection** questions.
- All answers must be found directly in or easily deduced from course book content.

**Figure 9** Multiple-Choice Example

- Multiple-choice questions are usually very specific with a single, clear answer.

## 34 Introduction: The Path to Certification

In the example question in **Figure 9**, you’re asked where in the system you can mark the **Reference field** on the journal entry header as a required entry. To answer this, you must know the configurations made for a **document type**, which is the correct answer.

**Figure 10** shows a sample **multiple-selection question** in which you must select two options as correct out of the four. This is a simple question with simple answer options because it’s testing knowledge of **system functions**, not of English. **SAP** avoids adding unneeded scenario information to a question; most of the time, every element of a question is important, so read the question carefully, and read the question twice to make sure you have it. There’s time, so don’t rush it.

### Figure 10 Multiple-Selection: Two Correct Out of Four

> **Note**  
> Another thing to keep in mind is that the test questions aren’t written to trick you. You can take the question at face value. There may be important details, but they aren’t designed to trip you up; instead, they are there to check that you comprehend a subject rather than just have it memorized.

In the **multiple-selection question**, you need to select both correct answer options to have the answer marked correct. **SAP** doesn’t give points for half a correct answer because it doesn’t deduct points for a wrong answer. The simple sample question here is correct when you select both the **Park** and **Post** answer options.

One level up the difficulty ladder is the multiple-selection question with **three correct options out of five**, as shown in **Figure 11**. One additional answer option adds one further parameter to consider and ultimately a greater chance of getting it wrong. It usually takes a bit longer just to read through it all and take it in.

The following question is used in this example:  
**Which of the following fields can you enter when creating or changing a general ledger account?**

When you’re sure of a field, then it’s correct; don’t overthink it. Marking down the ones you’re sure of leaves you with a simpler question. You know one answer is correct, so you now have a two-out-of-four question instead of a two-out-of-five question. If you know two answers for sure, then you’re left with a one-out-of-three question.

It seems obvious, but **eliminating options** is the best way to get them out of mind and out of sight. Concentrate on the real dilemma; don’t keep going over the ones you know. The same goes for wrong answer options. Writing convincing wrong answers is challenging, so take advantage of this: when something looks out of place, know that it probably is.

Eliminating one answer from the possible correct options leaves you with **three correct out of four**, which is much easier. If the **direct knowledge approach** doesn’t work, go ahead with the **process of elimination**. Knowing what is incorrect is as important as knowing what is correct for the certification.

### Figure 11 Multiple-Selection: Three Correct Out of Five

You’ll have **three hours** to go through all exam questions. This gives you a little over **two minutes per question**. Questions are designed to be readable in **30 seconds or less** on average, so that should leave you plenty of time to go through the full exam.

Stay relaxed and don’t worry about the time; concentrate on the question at hand, and if you’re unsure of the answer, move on. The system keeps track of questions that haven’t been answered. Before submitting the exam as final, always answer all questions to the best of your ability.

There is **no penalty for wrong answers**, so submitting no answer is a wasted chance at an educated guess. **SAP** allows you to retake a certification exam **up to three times**. Both the order of the questions and the order of the answers in a question are randomized. In other words, you won’t get new questions if you retake the same exam, but the questions will be mixed.

## Tips and Tricks

The following are some useful tips to use when preparing for the exam:

- Bulleted lists in materials are a great resource for creating questions, especially multiple-selection questions, so always keep your eyes open for them.
- Use the assessment questions in the materials and in this book to gauge your understanding of a topic. If you don’t understand something, reread the relevant section, check the correct answer details, and, if needed, ask a question in an online forum or community.
- There’s a lot of content to cover, so give yourself the time required to study all of it. You won’t be able to review all the information the night before the exam, so it’s better to invest in a good night’s sleep rather than another review cycle.
- Get to the exam center or be ready for the cloud examination early. Remove as many additional stress factors as possible; being late shouldn’t be something you should have to worry about.
- Avoid or at least don’t put too much stock into answering “certification” questions outside official **SAP** resources. These are usually badly written and many times answered incorrectly. The **SAP Training and Adoption** courses (and this book) give you plenty to work with.

### During the Exam

- Answer **all questions**, and bookmark the questions you’re unsure of to revisit them. This allows you to focus on specific ones instead of wasting time on selections you made confidently.
- Experience has shown that your **initial selection** is usually better than a revised one. Be cautious of going back over questions and answers too many times.
- Don’t worry too much about time. In most cases, you’ll be able to go over the questions **two or three times** if you want to.
- You don’t have to get it all correct. Don’t stress out because you hit two or three questions in a row of which you’re unsure.
- Try to rationalize and keep your cool. Read the question a couple times, and confirm you understand the question by restating it in your own words.
- Then move to the answer options and read through all of them thoroughly. Even if it’s multiple-choice and you identify the right answer, always read all answer options.
- Eliminate the answer options that don’t make sense or are obviously wrong. Usually, one of the wrong answers sticks out as incorrect, and the fewer options you have, the better your chance of selecting the right one.
- In some cases, there might be answer options that are **paired**; that is, if one answer is correct, then the other must be wrong. Because both can’t be correct, you must select one of the two in any case.
- Questions might look similar or might cover the same topic. Although **SAP** avoids having too many questions that overlap, it does happen. Watch out for the differentiators in the question and the answer options, and treat them as new questions.

## Additional Learning Resources

Undoubtedly, gaining the knowledge to pass the certification exam is important; a **certification** is valuable in the job marketplace, and it does verify at least a certain level of knowledge. However, in the IT field especially, **innovation never stands still**; plus, the sheer scope of the **SAP product offerings**, even just for financial accounting, is truly awe-inspiring.

Not strictly for preparation of a certification, but in the general scope of learning more about different areas and keeping your knowledge up to date, the following subsections provide a few useful resources for you to consider.

### Stay-Current Materials

These materials are created and provided by **SAP Training and Adoption** in direct cooperation with the development departments that build the solutions. **Stay-current materials** are released and made available on the **SAP Learning Hub** (requires a valid license) for every major product release on the day the product is released to customers.

For on-premise **SAP S/4HANA**, a new set of learning programs is created at least annually (**Figure 12** shows the learning programs made available for **SAP S/4HANA 2020**) and updated as needed to include features released with every new feature and service packs throughout the year.

### Figure 12 Stay-Current Materials for SAP S/4HANA 2020

With stay-current programs, you get access to live and recorded webinars, information for useful links, and presentations of what is new, how new features work, and how to implement the new features in the system.

The content is **delta** in nature by default, so it’s ideal to continue to stay current on new functionality after you gain a baseline knowledge from **SAP’s full-scale education courses**. The education courses will take a subset of what’s new to filter back into the core learning curriculum, and sometimes features or functions are large and important enough to warrant a completely new course.

### SAP Best Practices Explorer

The **SAP S/4HANA** system deployment and the **SAP Activate methodology** is closely integrated with **SAP Best Practices**. A new system will generally use a best practices package as the baseline on which a customer will build its own processes (or in some cases, the customer will change its processes to match the best practices).

Through **SAP Best Practices Explorer** ([https://rapid.sap.com/bp](https://rapid.sap.com/bp); see **Figure 13**), you can access detailed definitions of the best practices solution scopes, test scripts detailing the steps to perform various business processes, and business process diagrams that graphically depict processes steps.

### Figure 13 SAP Best Practices Explorer for SAP S/4HANA 2020

### SAP Help Portal

The **SAP Help Portal** ([https://help.sap.com](https://help.sap.com); see **Figure 14**) is an additional go-to place for finding detailed information on **SAP** products.

### Figure 14 SAP Help Portal

Especially for **administration information**, it offers a wealth of details. With every release of **SAP S/4HANA**, you can expect the following documents to be made available:

- **What’s new viewer**  
  Offers a complete overview of the new features and functions in every new release of SAP S/4HANA.

- **Feature scope description**  
  Provides an overview of the available features.

- **Installation guide**  
  Helps you install SAP S/4HANA.

- **Upgrade guide**  
  Describes the upgrade process to different software versions.

- **Conversion guide**  
  Supports the conversion from SAP ERP to SAP S/4HANA.

- **UI technologies guide**  
  Gives information on the user interface (**UI**) implementation.

- **Security guide**  
  Enables the implementation of a secure system landscape.

- **Operations guide**  
  Helps you operate your system.

- **Simplification list**  
  Describes features that aren’t in scope for SAP S/4HANA in comparison to SAP ERP and provides alternatives.

### SAP Product Assistance

The **SAP Help Portal** has a link to **Product Assistance** (refer to the lower middle of the screen in **Figure 14**). This is what was formally known as the **SAP Library**, and it has information for each application and many processes in SAP S/4HANA, including **configuration steps**.

**Figure 15** shows a page with details on **General Ledger Accounting (FI-GL)**; on the left, you can see the tree menu with details for each area of the same.

### Figure 15 Product Assistance

### SAP User Enablement Videos

The user enablement videos created by **SAP** for **SAP Enable Now** showcase basic best practices tasks performed in an actual system environment. These can be a great way for people without access to an **SAP S/4HANA** system to understand how the business processes are executed within the system using the **SAP Fiori** interface.

## SAP Fiori Apps Reference Library

The **SAP Fiori apps reference library** is an extremely important resource for you to keep an eye on ([http://s-prs.co/485601](http://s-prs.co/485601)). Here you’ll see every app made available for **SAP Fiori**. 

- Quickly find newly released apps and apps that have changed.
- For native **SAP Fiori apps**, find a short description of their functionality.
- For all apps, get analytical details of how to configure them in your system.

In Figure 16, you can see an example for the **Monitor Payments app**, in which the application details can be viewed for the different product releases (**SAP S/4HANA, SAP S/4HANA Cloud, SAP ERP**, etc.). 

In the search box, you can filter via many parameters, such as **LOB**, product, release, and more.

---

## SAP Community

The **SAP Community** is another great way to gain valuable knowledge and get assistance from other expert community members ([http://s-prs.co/485602](http://s-prs.co/485602); see Figure 17).

- Contains many blog posts with useful **how-to guides**.
- Plenty of questions have already been answered.

---

## openSAP

**openSAP** is SAP’s free massive open online course (**MOOC**) enterprise offering (Figure 18). 

- Offers a wealth of ongoing and previously run courses on topics like **machine learning, big data, Internet of Things (IoT)**, and more.
- Limited content for **financial accounting** specifically.
- Courses do not go into very deep detail, making it a fantastic resource for keeping up with the latest innovations and trends without prior knowledge.

# Chapter 1  
## Overview and Deployment of SAP S/4HANA

### Techniques You’ll Master

- Explain the **SAP strategy for digital transformation**.
- Describe the **SAP framework for the digital enterprise**.
- Understand the role of the **SAP Business Technology Platform** and **intelligent technologies**.
- Review basic **SAP HANA technology**.
- Describe the scope of **financials for SAP S/4HANA**.
- Choose the relevant **deployment option for SAP S/4HANA**.
- Explain the **SAP Fiori design pillars**.
- Use the **SAP Fiori launchpad**.
- Describe the basic **SAP Fiori app types**.

---

In this chapter, we’ll explore the architecture of **SAP HANA**, describe the scope and deployment options of **SAP S/4HANA**, and discuss the basic functions of the **SAP Fiori user interface (UI)**.

### Real-World Scenario

As a consultant, you need to understand the underlying architecture that the **SAP S/4HANA system** is built on.

- **SAP HANA** is at the core of the SAP strategy.
- The technology is a faster database with features such as **compression** and **columnar store**.
- It is important to explain these technical aspects in simple terms to nontechnical customers.
- The **SAP S/4HANA system** is a separate product line from the old **SAP ERP system**.
- SAP ERP is no longer the default go-to **enterprise resource planning (ERP)** platform.
- Customers can be persuaded by the true benefits of the new system but may have concerns about adopting it.
- Consultants must explain SAP’s reasons for this move and what it means for existing customers.
- **SAP Fiori** is the default graphical user interface (**GUI**) for end users in **SAP S/4HANA**.
- You must be able to confidently use **SAP Fiori**, explain its components, and describe its benefits.
- Emphasize the importance of simple interfaces with excellent usability that work on both **mobile devices** and **desktops**.
- Understand how **tile groups**, **tile catalogs**, **roles**, and **users** cooperate to form the **SAP Fiori launchpad**.

---

### 1.1 Objectives of This Portion of the Test

The certification exam portion tests your general knowledge of:

- Overview of **SAP HANA in-memory architecture**
- **SAP S/4HANA products** and architecture for **financials**
- Deployment options for **SAP S/4HANA**
- **SAP Fiori launchpad** features
- **SAP Fiori app** types

> **Note:** The SAP HANA and SAP S/4HANA topic makes up **10%** of the total exam.

---

### 1.2 Digital Transformation

Because technological change is accelerating, businesses must not only catch up but also leverage technology to gain competitive advantage.

- Computers and software traditionally support business.
- **Digital transformation** brings digital technology to the forefront as a key **business driver**.
- It involves adopting technologies such as **big data**, **Internet of Things (IoT)**, **mobile**, **artificial intelligence (AI)**, and **social media**.
- These technologies enable **business innovation** and **growth**.

---

### 1.3 Intelligent Enterprise Framework

Digital transformation impacts all business functions:

- Marketing
- Operations
- Human resources
- Administration, etc.

It forces organizations to rethink and optimize business processes and embrace **automation**.

SAP’s strategic framework to support the **intelligent enterprise** focuses on three key product offerings:

#### Intelligent Suite

- Includes all SAP applications that support **end-to-end business processes** (see Figure 1.1).

#### Digital Platform

- Refers to the **SAP Business Technology Platform**, an open platform for building and delivering business applications.
- SAP is shifting development focus from core solutions into the **SAP Business Technology Platform** to ensure flexibility for SAP and third-party developers while keeping the core lean.

#### Intelligent Technologies

- Formerly under the **SAP Leonardo** umbrella.
- Combines modern tools that improve applications by providing **automation**, **detection**, and **prevention**.
- Key technologies include **process automation**, **AI**, **machine learning**, **blockchain**, **data intelligence**, **big data**, **IoT**, and **predictive analytics**.

Traditional ERP software does not fully support digital transformation. SAP created **SAP HANA** to be the core building block that drives this transformation and is now central to all SAP product development.

---

### 1.3.1 SAP HANA Architecture

At its core, **SAP HANA** is a **database management system** with unique features:

- Performs all expected database functions such as storing and retrieving data for applications.
- Embedded **advanced analytics** capabilities: **predictive analytics, text analysis, mining, search**.
- Application development services for multiple programming languages.
- Provides data access, administration, and security services.

We focus here on the database architecture relevant for certification and the financial accounting associate role.

The SAP HANA database has three standout features:

#### In-Memory Database

- Uses **RAM** to store all data, which is much faster than disk storage.
- Modern memory reads/writes at about **60 GB/s**, compared to disk drives at about **3 GB/s**, a factor of 20 difference.
- This technology is more expensive, but costs are usually manageable for enterprises.
- Memory size limitations are mitigated by other SAP HANA features.

#### Aggressive Compression

- While all databases support compression, it often sacrifices speed.
- SAP HANA uses smart techniques to compress data on average by a factor of **10** with minimal speed loss.
- Avoids the expensive decompress/recompress cycle by **inserting only new data** rather than editing existing entries.
- Uses a **versioning system** to always read the latest data entry without decompressing old entries.

## Columnar Data Storage

**SAP HANA** uses the **columnar data store type** for two major reasons:  
- Much better **compression**  
- Faster **data retrieval** for queries (when only a subset of the full table data set is required)  

**Column storage** works great for **data aggregation** (SAP HANA is used for ad hoc aggregation a lot) and **parallel processing**. It is more common in **online analytical processing (OLAP)** applications (e.g., business warehouse systems) rather than **online transactional processing (OLTP)** systems (typical ERP systems), where row storage is considered faster. Although SAP HANA supports both types of tables, developers can decide what works for their use case. However, the **columnar store** is where SAP HANA shines.

---

## 1.3.2 Technology Enablers for Success with SAP HANA

Most databases are designed to work optimally with the technology available at the time of their design. Prior to SAP HANA, applications minimized **disk access** and performed calculations in the code. As technology progresses, this design approach is no longer the only way.

The main **technology drivers and trends** behind SAP's investment in SAP HANA include:

- **Large-volume, extremely high-bandwidth, affordable memory**  
  Memory has always been faster, but purchasing and utilizing such volumes was inconceivable 20 years ago.

- **New-generation microprocessors with multiple cores and larger optimized caches**  
  CPUs can now access data at much higher rates than before.

- **Expandable modular data centers**  
  These can now be expanded by adding servers for more memory and processing power to meet sizing requirements.

- **Cloud computing applications**  
  Used increasingly by customers as alternatives to on-premise software, including critical backend components. Cloud saves IT costs, ensures solutions are up to date, offers transparent cost of ownership through subscription models, and increases flexibility.

---

## 1.4 SAP S/4HANA

**SAP S/4HANA** is the current **ERP solution** from SAP, optimized exclusively for **SAP HANA**. Unlike previous SAP ERP solutions, it only works on SAP HANA.

SAP S/4HANA consists of:  
- The **SAP S/4HANA Enterprise Management digital core**, closest in scope to the SAP ERP solution  
- Various **line of business (LoB) solutions**, mostly cloud solutions gained through mergers and acquisitions, optimized for seamless integration  

### Figure 1.2 SAP S/4HANA: Digital Core

### Main Line of Business (LoB) Solutions:  
- **SAP C/4HANA**: Customer experience and engagement suite  
- **SAP SuccessFactors** and **SAP Fieldglass**: Human resource management  
- **SAP Concur**: Travel management  
- **SAP Ariba**: Sourcing and procurement  

---

### Goals of SAP S/4HANA

1. **Writing code to take advantage of SAP HANA**  
   SAP simplified and sped up system architecture by removing redundancies such as:  
   - Aggregation tables (totals are calculated on the fly from line items)  
   - Index tables used for reporting (SAP HANA’s speed allows direct line-item level queries)  
   - Removal of indices to reduce code complexity  

2. **Safeguarding existing customer investments**  
   SAP uses **compatibility views** to replicate obsolete tables on the fly, allowing legacy programs to continue functioning. Customers can transform their SAP ERP systems to SAP S/4HANA with minimal downtime.

### Figure 1.3 SAP HANA Application Simplification

- Legacy applications rely on **compatibility views**, aggregates, and index tables.  
- SAP HANA-optimized applications read directly from **line-item tables**, simplifying data access.

**Note:**  
The first simplified SAP ERP component was **Financial Accounting** with the introduction of the **universal ledger** in **SAP Simple Finance 1503** (internally called **SFIN2.0**). The financial-only SAP S/4HANA was once a separate product but is now part of the complete SAP S/4HANA suite.

---

## 1.4.1 SAP S/4HANA Deployment Options

There are three SAP S/4HANA deployment options as detailed in **Table 1.1**:

### Simplified Editions from a Functional Consultant Perspective:

- **SAP S/4HANA Cloud (Private Edition)**  
  - Slightly limited scope and customization (scope parity aimed by end of 2021)  

- **SAP S/4HANA (Any-Premise Edition)**  
  - Full functionality and configuration flexibility  
  - Can be deployed on-premise or cloud infrastructure with the same features  

### Table 1.1 SAP S/4HANA Deployment Options

| Feature                 | SAP S/4HANA Cloud, Public Edition | SAP S/4HANA Cloud, Private Edition | SAP S/4HANA Any-Premise      |
|-------------------------|----------------------------------|-----------------------------------|-----------------------------|
| Innovation lifecycle    | Quarterly                        | Semiannual                       | Annual, customer-led         |
| Total cost of ownership (TCO) | Lowest                            | Lower                            | Higher                      |
| System governance      | SAP-led                         | Customer-influenced             | Customer-led                |
| IT infrastructure      | SAP, public                    | SAP, dedicated                  | Customer-managed            |
| Customization          | Within standards               | Within standards                | Open to modifications       |
| Extension              | Platform as a service (PaaS), SAP BTP | PaaS, SAP BTP                  | Open, SAP BTP               |
| System delivery        | New implementation             | New implementation              | New or SAP ERP conversion   |

**Warning:**  
The **any-premise edition** was referred to as **on-premise** in previous SAP S/4HANA releases. This certification and book focus on the any-premise edition.

---

## 1.4.2 SAP S/4HANA Adoption

Customers have four major options to start using SAP S/4HANA:

### New Implementation

- Also known as the **greenfield approach**.  
- Customers move from legacy (SAP ERP or non-SAP) systems to SAP S/4HANA from scratch.  
- Preferred by customers with highly customized ERP solutions wanting a fresh start.  
- Available for all SAP S/4HANA editions.

### System Conversion

- Converts existing SAP ERP systems into SAP S/4HANA.  
- Allows migration without reimplementation or major disruption.  
- Businesses can gradually adopt SAP S/4HANA and SAP Fiori processes afterward.  
- Available for on-premise and private cloud editions.

**Tip:**  
Financial accounting consultants' tasks during system conversion are part of the **SAP Certified Application Professional – Financials in SAP S/4HANA** certification, but out of scope for the application associate certification.

### Landscape Transformation

- Consolidates multiple diverse ERP landscapes into a single SAP S/4HANA system.  
- Typically done gradually, not in a single step.  
- Works on-premise and may selectively work with cloud deployment.

### Central Finance

- Enables a gradual move to SAP S/4HANA, keeping source ERP systems intact.  
- Most transactions remain in source systems; data replicates into a central SAP S/4HANA system.  
- Utilizes the **Universal Journal** and SAP S/4HANA reporting functionality.

---

## 1.4.3 SAP S/4HANA System Landscape

System landscapes vary by customer requirements and legacy systems. A typical new SAP S/4HANA installation requires two productive systems:

- **SAP S/4HANA backend server** (required for ERP system)  
- **SAP Gateway server** (establishes connections and settings for SAP Fiori)

Both systems can be accessed via the traditional **SAP GUI**.

### Figure 1.4 SAP Logon Screen with SAP S/4HANA Backend and SAP Gateway Server

- Example from SAP Training:  
  - **T41** is the backend server  
  - **T4N** is the gateway server  

**Note:**  
While theoretically optional, **SAP Fiori** is essential for fully utilizing SAP S/4HANA. Performing a system conversion without implementing SAP Fiori should be seen as the initial step towards adoption.

---

## 1.5 SAP Fiori User Interface

**SAP Fiori** is the common design paradigm for SAP—affecting the look and feel of all SAP products, not just the SAP S/4HANA interface.

## SAP Fiori User Interface

SAP recognized that **everyday apps** are becoming **simpler to use** and more **flexible**. Business software needs to keep up with this development, or else the disconnect between "work software" and "daily apps" will cause issues in **user acceptance**, **satisfaction**, and **productivity**.

To create apps in **SAP Fiori**, you use the **SAPUI5 framework**. This framework is based on the open-source **OpenUI5 framework**, with the addition of a few extra **SAP-specific tools**. **SAPUI5** is an **open-source framework**, meaning anyone can use it and implement improvements. The main development tools for **SAPUI5** include **HTML5**, **CSS3**, **jQuery**, and **JavaScript**. Basing the entire development platform on **open standards** ensures that many people are familiar with the tools needed to develop SAP Fiori apps and that the apps have great compatibility across multiple device platforms.

---

## 1.5.1 SAP Fiori User Experience Paradigm

The **SAP Fiori design and user experience paradigm** is built on **five principles**:

- **Role-based**  
  Applications should focus on providing the functionality required for a **specific task**. Complex screens with infinite selection options and one app for doing everything is not the aim.

- **Responsive**  
  Apps should be usable on **multiple devices** and able to adjust their interface to fit the **device size**, **input methods**, and so on.

- **Simple**  
  Apps should require **no manual** or **special training** to be used. They should be designed for a single user and use case and require **no more than three screens** end-to-end.

- **Coherent**  
  The design should be **consistent** between apps, so users feel **instant familiarity** when accessing new apps. Apps should also have **technical coherence**, meaning they can be ported to other systems and use the same language.

- **Instant Value**  
  Apps need to be **useful immediately**, meaning they should be easy to **install**, **configure**, and **deploy**. Users should clearly understand the app's purpose and not need help or training after seeing a couple of SAP Fiori apps.

---

## 1.5.2 SAP Fiori for SAP S/4HANA

**SAP Fiori for SAP S/4HANA** refers to the apps available for the system. The SAP development teams continuously develop **native apps** for SAP Fiori to replace the traditional and often "busier" **SAP GUI apps** inherited by SAP S/4HANA.

**Native apps** can leverage new technologies such as **conversational UI**, **machine learning**, **immersive experiences**, and more. SAP S/4HANA Finance already has many native apps available.

In addition to native SAP Fiori apps, **SAP GUI apps** can be launched from the **SAP Fiori launchpad**. These apps run in a web browser with an **SAP Fiori look and feel** (see Figure 1.5). The large scope of **SAP ERP apps** means not all apps need to be replaced at once, giving SAP room to create useful and simpler native apps without sacrificing coverage.

Customers can also develop their own apps. Adding SAP GUI apps to SAP Fiori allows legacy **custom ABAP apps** to work through SAP Fiori.

### Example Design Elements for SAP Fiori-Look Classic Apps (Figure 1.5)

1. A **text-based toolbar** instead of icons  
2. All **labels right-aligned**  
3. **Condensed table rows**  
4. New **design icons** with a common design language  
5. The **SAP logo** and buttons in the SAP Fiori header replace in-app navigation controls  
6. Redesigned **tab strips** (active tab highlighting)  
7. Processing and closing actions moved to the **footer** of the screen

> **Tip:** SAP GUI apps are referred to as **SAP S/4HANA classic applications**.

---

## SAP Fiori App Categories

SAP Fiori apps fit into three categories:

- **Transactional apps**  
  Used to perform operations such as master record creation, maintenance, or posting transactions.  
  *Example:* Clear Incoming Payments (Figure 1.6).

- **Analytical apps**  
  Detailed reports used to drill down to finer details or zoom out to an organization level.  
  *Example:* Overdue Receivables (Figure 1.7).

- **Factsheet apps**  
  Quick overviews of a specific object with basic details and key performance indicators (KPIs) in one screen. Navigation is usually possible between related factsheets.  
  *Example:* Supplier Invoice Search (Figure 1.8).

SAP offers more than **2,000 native apps** built for SAP Fiori and over **9,000 classic SAP GUI and Web Dynpro apps** accessible through the SAP Fiori landscape. Additionally, SAP provides more than **500 standard business roles** preconfigured for user assignment. These can be used as templates or combined in custom roles.

---

## 1.5.3 SAP Fiori Launchpad

The **SAP Fiori launchpad** is the **user access point** to the system (Figure 1.9). It is a **customizable web-based interface** from which all assigned apps can be launched. Apps do not need to be from one specific system; tiles can launch apps and links for any connected and compatible system.

### Important Characteristics and Functionalities

- Accessed from a **web browser** with a fixed URL that can be shared across the network. Authorized users log in without needing local software installation.

- Apps are displayed as **tiles** (or sometimes text links). Tiles can be:
  - **Static**: fixed icon  
  - **Active**: show important information directly without clicking, updating periodically.  
  *Examples:* Open payments, open workflow messages (Figure 1.10).

- The **advanced search functionality** can search for many characteristics and display info directly in a factsheet (Figure 1.11).

- End users can **customize apps and app groups** on the launchpad. Selecting **Edit Homepage** lets users reposition, remove, add apps, and modify groups. Users can reset groups to default anytime (Figure 1.12).

> **Warning:** The scope of apps, initial grouping, and included apps are controlled by an **administrator**.

- Users can save the current app view (including inputs) as a **new tile** for quick access (Figure 1.13). Especially useful for KPI reports with specific characteristic combinations.

- SAP Fiori provides a **context help menu** accessible via a **question mark icon** in the launchpad header. The menu offers general help, field explanations, and sometimes video tutorials (Figure 1.14).

- Customers can fully **customize the look and feel** of the launchpad using their own themes. Colors, backgrounds, logos, fonts, etc. can be changed via the **UI Theme Designer** (Figure 1.15).

- The **Settings** option in the user menu displays user account info (Figure 1.16). Here users select themes, default language and region, enable customized searches, clear search cache, and set default values for system attributes like company code and plant.

---

## 1.5.4 SAP Fiori Launchpad Designer

In **SAP S/4HANA**, you define **roles** that provide **authorizations** for various functions and assign these roles to users. A user can have multiple roles.

SAP delivers a standard set of roles and sample users through **SAP Best Practices content**. These business roles contain SAP Fiori **tile catalogs** and **tile groups**.

- **Catalogs and groups** are assigned to roles.  
- Roles assigned to users define which tiles a user sees on the launchpad, can add to groups, and can launch via the app finder.

You can use SAP-delivered standard catalogs and groups or customize your own. The **SAP Fiori launchpad designer** lets you create catalogs and groups for the SAP Fiori launchpad (Figure 1.17).

**SAP Fiori catalogs** hold configuration info for apps, such as names, subtitles, icons, and technical tile settings.

---

© 2024 by Rheinwerk Publishing Inc., Boston (MA)

## SAP Fiori Catalogs and Roles

After you’ve created a **catalog**, you assign it to a **role** (and the role to a user). The **application tiles** inside the catalog define the applications a user has access to. If a tile is included in an **SAP Fiori tile group** to which a user is assigned, but the tile isn’t in any of the catalogs assigned, the user won’t be able to see the tile. You’ll need to assign the **catalog** to the user that the tile is in.

You can create as many **catalogs** as required to meet the needs of end-user roles (see Figure 1.18).

**Figure 1.18** SAP Fiori Launchpad Designer: Catalogs

The name of a **group** and the tiles included in that group are assigned in the **SAP Fiori tile group configuration** in the **SAP Fiori launchpad designer** (see Figure 1.19). You can add tiles to the group from many different catalogs, but the user must be assigned to all the relevant catalogs to see and use the tiles.

You can select whether the end user will be allowed to change a tile group on his own launchpad or not. Finally, you select whether apps will be displayed as **tiles** or as **links**.

> **Warning**  
> If you make changes to **SAP-delivered catalogs or groups**, these will be overwritten by updated versions of the groups and catalogs provided by SAP. It’s always best to create your own and assign tiles as needed. You can then assign these to your own roles.

**Figure 1.19** SAP Fiori Launchpad Designer: Groups

---

## 1.6 Important Terminology

In this chapter, the following terminology was used:

- **Columnar store**  
  Data is stored in **columns** instead of in the more traditional **rows**; this allows speedier **read performance** and greater **compression capabilities**. The downside is **suboptimal transactional processing**.

- **In-memory technology**  
  Data storage in **RAM** instead of in disks to capitalize on lower **latency** and **read/write times**. The technology still makes use of disks for historic data and backup purposes.

- **Intelligent technologies**  
  Technological frameworks that are used in conjunction with **SAP Business Technology Platform** to develop **next-generation applications**. Relevant technologies include **machine learning, IoT, process automation, predictive analytics, blockchain, data intelligence, and big data**.

- **SAP Business Technology Platform**  
  A **development and deployment platform** that aids in the creation of **intelligent, integrated, and mobile-ready applications** to support business operations.

- **SAP Fiori**  
  A new common design paradigm for all SAP applications. The design goal is to make **business apps intuitive** to use and available on all platforms and devices. **SAP Fiori** is based on the following design principles: **role-based, responsive, simple, coherent, and instant value**.

- **SAP Fiori for SAP S/4HANA**  
  A group of applications that are designed for **SAP S/4HANA**. There are three basic app types: **transactional, analytical, and factsheet**.

- **SAP Fiori launchpad**  
  The UI “cockpit” for SAP Fiori that is accessed through any modern **web browser** without extra software requirements. It displays several applications in flat, rectangular forms called **tiles**. The applications available depend on the user’s **role and authorizations**. The **SAP Fiori launchpad** offers many **Customizing options** for the end user, such as **theme selection, custom grouping, and displayed application selection**.

- **SAP Fiori launchpad designer**  
  Administrator interface to customize the **catalogs** and **groups** available in the system. You define the configuration for SAP Fiori tiles in the **Catalog section** and for the tiles included in groups in the **Group section**.

- **SAP Gateway server**  
  The server used to connect SAP Fiori to one or more **SAP S/4HANA, SAP ERP, SAP Business Warehouse (SAP BW)**, and other backend systems. **SAP Fiori app configuration** is performed here, as well as **SAP Fiori user maintenance**.

- **SAP S/4HANA**  
  The new **ERP system** from SAP that leverages **SAP HANA** to simplify the code and data structures. It’s designed to be the **digital core** for all business applications of the customer and to allow businesses to **go digital**. It’s offered **on premise** with a traditional ownership model and in the **cloud** with a subscription model.

---

## 1.7 Practice Questions

These practice questions will help you evaluate your understanding of the topics covered in this chapter. The questions shown are similar to those found on the **certification examination**.

Select the correct answers, and then check the completeness of your answers in the next section. Remember that, on the exam, you must select **all correct answers** and **only correct answers** to receive credit for the question.

1. Which SAP technological products provide the platform required for SAP to support the digital transformation of an organization? (**Two correct answers**)
   - A. **SAP HANA**
   - B. SAP Data Intelligence
   - C. SAP Fiori
   - D. **SAP Business Technology Platform**

2. You want to develop a substantial enhancement for the purchase-to-pay process in your SAP S/4HANA system. Where does SAP recommend you perform this enhancement?  
   - A. SAP Analytics Cloud  
   - B. SAP Fiori  
   - C. **SAP Business Technology Platform**  
   - D. SAP S/4HANA core

3. True or False: SAP S/4HANA (on premise) can be deployed on a cloud infrastructure.  
   - A. **True**  
   - B. False

4. The SAP HANA database relies on which of the following technologies for storing data? (**Three correct answers**)
   - A. **In-memory**  
   - B. Aggregation  
   - C. Indexing  
   - D. **Columnar store**  
   - E. **Compression**

5. Data in the SAP HANA database is stored in which two ways? (**Two correct answers**)  
   - A. Random  
   - B. Vector  
   - C. **Column**  
   - D. **Row**

6. True or False: In an environment of systems using SAP HANA, you can perform both OLAP and OLTP processing without duplication of the data for the SAP BW and SAP ERP systems.  
   - A. **True**  
   - B. False

7. SAP HANA makes extensive use of which high-speed hardware technology to offer more speed?  
   - A. Read-only memory  
   - B. Solid-state drives (SSDs)  
   - C. Graphics processing units (GPUs)  
   - D. **Multicore CPUs**

8. True or False: SAP S/4HANA replaces SAP ERP, and development and support are shifted completely to it.  
   - A. True  
   - B. **False**

9. Which product line does the SAP S/4HANA system rely on for procurement functions?  
   - A. SAP Concur  
   - B. SAP SuccessFactors  
   - C. **SAP Ariba**  
   - D. SAP C/4HANA

10. What technology did SAP leverage to eliminate aggregate tables from the SAP S/4HANA system while maintaining compatibility with many legacy programs?  
    - A. Columnar store  
    - B. **Compatibility views**  
    - C. Data aging  
    - D. Indices

11. True or False: Choosing between SAP S/4HANA and SAP S/4HANA Cloud, public edition, is also a matter of required scope and Customizing flexibility.  
    - A. **True**  
    - B. False

12. True or False: The only version of the SAP S/4HANA Cloud, public edition, a customer can be on is the latest released version.  
    - A. **True**  
    - B. False

13. A user wants to add an app to his SAP Fiori homepage but can’t find it in the app finder. What does the admin have to do?  
    - A. Assign the corresponding SAP Fiori tile group to the user.  
    - B. **Assign the corresponding SAP Fiori tile catalog to the user.**  
    - C. Add the tile to a tile group already assigned to the user.  
    - D. Add the corresponding tile catalog to the tile group.

14. Where can an SAP Fiori end user change the theme of his SAP Fiori launchpad?  
    - A. **In the User Menu of the SAP Fiori launchpad**  
    - B. In the Tile Catalog area of the SAP Fiori launchpad designer  
    - C. In the Tile Group area of the SAP Fiori launchpad designer  
    - D. In the UI theme designer

15. True or False: Anyone with an appropriate user name and password can log on to the SAP Fiori launchpad through a web browser.  
    - A. True  
    - B. **False**

16. What kind of customizations can users make to their SAP Fiori launchpads? (**Two correct answers**)  
    - A. **Change the name of tile groups.**  
    - B. **Create their own tile groups.**  
    - C. Change the names of tiles.  
    - D. Change the icons on tiles.

17. Which of the following are SAP Fiori design principles? (**Two correct answers**)  
    - A. **Role-based**  
    - B. Routine  
    - C. Rational  
    - D. **Responsive**

18. You use the search in your SAP Fiori launchpad to look up information for a cost center. What kind of app is used for the information shown in the search results?  
    - A. Transactional  
    - B. **Factsheet**  
    - C. Analytical  
    - D. List

## 1.8 Practice Question Answers and Explanations

1. Correct answers: **A, D**  
**SAP HANA** is SAP’s default platform to support the **digital transformation** for businesses. In addition, the **SAP Business Technology Platform** provides the infrastructure and tools for developing **next-generation applications**.

2. Correct answer: **C**  
Traditionally, such enhancements are made directly in the core SAP ERP component. This will indeed still work today in your SAP S/4HANA system; however, SAP wants to shift such development to the **SAP Business Technology Platform**. This strategy keeps the core running lean and close to standard. SAP Analytics Cloud is for planning and reporting; SAP Fiori represents the UI level and not where enhancement development happens.

3. Correct answer: **A**  
True. There is no limitation on the location of the hardware that the on-premise version of **SAP S/4HANA** is deployed on. Customers can choose third-party cloud vendors or SAP cloud infrastructure (called SAP S/4HANA Cloud, private edition).

4. Correct answers: **A, D, E**  
**In-memory**, **columnar store**, and **compression** are key SAP HANA storage technologies. Aggregates should be avoided to maintain data granularity. Indices offer little improvement and reduce reporting flexibility.

5. Correct answers: **C, D**  
Data is stored in **column** and **row** formats. Column store is preferred for reading data; row storage is supported fully.

6. Correct answer: **A**  
True. SAP HANA combines **OLTP** and **OLAP** processing in one database simplifying data management and IT resources.

7. Correct answer: **D**  
SAP HANA uses **multicore CPUs** to handle the high processing demands efficiently. GPUs also offer powerful calculations but CPUs are key.

8. Correct answer: **B**  
False. SAP **S/4HANA** does not fully replace SAP ERP in all contexts; some forms of development and support continue in SAP ERP.

---

*(The rest of the answers are omitted here for brevity but should be included similarly in the full formatted document.)*

## SAP HANA and Related Technologies

Although many companies consider using some of their special characteristics in the **business application world**, these are not currently used by **SAP HANA**. 

- **SSDs** offer a big boost to traditional databases, and since **SAP HANA** uses disk drives for many non-speed-critical processes (e.g., backup and aged data), they can be used with **SAP HANA**.
- They don’t offer much in speed improvement due to the architecture.
- **Read-only memory** is irrelevant to **SAP HANA**.

---

## SAP S/4HANA and SAP ERP

- **SAP S/4HANA** is the successor to **SAP ERP**, but it does **not** replace it.
- A large customer base still relies on **SAP ERP**, with support promised until **2027** (at the time of publication).

---

## SAP Product Overview

- **SAP Ariba** supports the **SAP S/4HANA digital core** with **procurement**.
- **SAP SuccessFactors** is for **human resources**.
- **SAP Concur** is for **travel management**.
- **SAP C/4HANA** supports everything around the **customer experience**.

---

## SAP HANA Compatibility and Views

- **Compatibility views** can be materialized on demand for data in **line-item tables** of the **SAP HANA database**.
- These views support programs that read old **aggregate and index tables** no longer in the system.

---

## SAP S/4HANA Product Scopes

- **SAP S/4HANA** offers a more complete solution with more customizing possibilities.
- The **SAP S/4HANA Cloud solution** suits new subsidiaries or companies wanting a lean digital core that is always up to date.
- The **private edition option** is basically equivalent to the any-premise edition, differing mostly in the licensing model (**perpetual** vs. **subscription licensing**).

---

## SAP S/4HANA Cloud Updates

- Quarterly updates for the **multitenant public cloud solution** are mandatory.
- Customers cannot skip product release cycles as the system upgrades simultaneously for all.
- Other editions allow more flexibility in upgrade paths and frequency.

---

## SAP Fiori Tile Catalog and Launchpad

- The **SAP Fiori tile catalog** defines which tiles a user is authorized to use.
- Without assignment to the right catalog, users won’t see the application tile even if it’s part of an assigned group.
- End users typically access only the **SAP Fiori launchpad**.
- The **user menu** controls all changeable settings for their **SAP Fiori launchpad**, including theme selection.

---

## SAP Fiori Usage and Customization

- No special software installation is needed; any modern web browser with **HTML5** support works.
- **Google Chrome** is recommended for better speed and compatibility.
- Changing the name and look of tiles can only be done in the **catalog view** of the **SAP Fiori launchpad designer**.
- **End users** can only manage their **tile groups** on the launchpad.

---

## SAP Fiori Principles

- Applications should be **role-based**, focusing on specific tasks of specific users.
- Apps should be **responsive**, adapting interfaces to work well on different devices.

---

## SAP Fiori App Types

- Search results display in a **factsheet app**, providing key facts for the searched object.
- Options include navigating to a **transactional app** (e.g., Manage Cost Centers) or an **analytical app** (e.g., cost center report).
- **List** is not an official app type in the **SAP Fiori design language**.

---

## 1.9 Test Takeaway

You now have an overview of the **SAP HANA database** and understand the benefits of its architecture and technologies improving traditional disk-based databases. You were introduced to the **SAP intelligent enterprise strategy** and the product portfolio supporting it, including:

- **SAP Business Technology Platform**
- **Intelligent technologies** (with **SAP HANA**, **SAP S/4HANA**, and cloud LoB solutions)

You gained a thorough introduction to **SAP S/4HANA**—the successor to **SAP ERP**—and its deployment options. You also learned about the **SAP Fiori design paradigm**, basic **SAP Fiori tools**, and how **tile catalogs and groups** control which apps users can see and use.

---

## 1.10 Summary

You have acquired a high-level understanding of:

- **SAP HANA**
- **SAP S/4HANA**
- **SAP Fiori**

You can explain their basic concepts and benefits, propose deployment options, and assist users with basic **SAP Fiori operations**. Although this chapter is technical and not directly related to **financial accounting in SAP S/4HANA**, it is vital knowledge for both new and experienced consultants.

The next chapter covers **General Ledger Accounting** business processes and customizing, beginning with core organizational units in **financial accounting** in **SAP S/4HANA**.

---

## Chapter 2: General Ledger Accounting

### Techniques You’ll Master

- Manage organizational units in **financial accounting**
- Maintain **general ledger master records**
- Configure **general ledger business processes**
- Understand **parallel valuation** and **document splitting** in **SAP S/4HANA**
- Configure headers and line items of **financial accounting documents**
- Understand **document posting** and **document editing options**

---

### Chapter Focus

This chapter explains **general ledger accounting** in the **SAP S/4HANA system**. Topics include:

- Configuration of basic **financial organizational units**
- Design and configuration of the **chart of accounts**
- Configuration of **general ledger master records**
- Document posting controls

---

### Real-World Scenario

As a **financial accounting consultant**, you translate customer requirements into system configuration. Knowing various available options is crucial, especially in **on-premise deployment**.

Many configuration decisions for the general ledger are difficult to change after the system goes live. Gaining confidence in building the right system is essential.

Whether specializing or generalizing in financial accounting, understanding the **general ledger configuration** is foundational. Almost all activities in **SAP S/4HANA** affect values in the general ledger.

Integration points require troubleshooting if unfamiliar with the general ledger component, impacting finance and other lines of business (**LoBs**).

The general ledger acts as the company’s window to the outside world. Correct, functional reporting is critical for trust.

In **SAP S/4HANA**, the general ledger is more integrated through the **Universal Journal**; all finance components update the same **line-item table** governed by general ledger design decisions.

---

### 2.1 Objectives of This Portion of the Test

This portion of the certification tests your understanding of:

- Customizing core organizational units and master records
- Main business processes of **general ledger accounting**

Consultants must understand:

- Definitions and possible assignments for organizational units in **financial accounting**
- Configuration and maintenance of **general ledger master records** (accounts, profit centers, segments)
- Configuration of **ledgers**, **document splitting**, and **currencies**
- Maintenance of the **chart of accounts** and general ledger master records
- Configuration of accounting documents including **document types**, **number ranges**, **posting authorizations**, and **period controls**
- Posting parameters such as **default values**, allowed changes, **reversal reasons**, **tax codes**, and **cross-company-code document posting**

> **Note:** The general ledger accounting topic constitutes **20%** of the exam.

---

### 2.2 Organizational Units

Organizational units in **SAP** represent real-life business entities in the system.

- Assigning organizational units to each other and underlying master records depicts the full enterprise.
- Business transactions reference specific organizational units.
- Reports analyze data at multiple levels and combinations of organizational units.

This section reviews the organizational units relevant to **financial accounting** and other main peripheral organizational units relevant by assignment and integration.

---

### 2.2.1 Client

- A **client** is the top-level organizational and legal entity in the **SAP system** hierarchy.
- **Organizational, master,** and **transactional data** are maintained at the client level.
- The client isolates data completely from other clients.
- Users log on by specifying a **client**.
- Clients segregate data into **client-dependent** and **client-independent**.

---

### SAP S/4HANA Clients

- An **SAP S/4HANA system (instance)** can have multiple clients (example in Figure 2.1).
- Base SAP instances include clients **000**, **001**, and **066**.
  - Client **066** is reserved for SAP use.
  - Client **000** contains base data but is generally unused in implementations.
  - Client **001** is a safety copy of **000**.
- System administrators mainly use **client 000** for maintenance and patching.
- Only administrators typically have access to **client 000**.

---

### Client Data Visibility

- Logging into **client 100** shows:
  - All **client-independent data** (e.g., ABAP programs)
  - All data dependent on **client 100** (organizational, master, transactional)

- Logging into **client 200** shows:
  - The same **client-independent data**
  - All data specific to **client 200**

This distinction ensures separation of **client-dependent** and **client-independent** data.

---

![Figure 2.1 SAP S/4HANA System with Multiple Clients](https://example.com/figure2.1)  
*Figure 2.1 SAP S/4HANA System with Multiple Clients*

## Client-Dependent and Client-Independent Data

In certain system tables, all rows are accessible from any client—such as the **Data Dictionary tables**, tables containing **ABAP programs**, printers, and so on—this is referred to as **client-independent data**. 

**Users, company codes, vendors, customers, and document line items** are all **client-dependent data**; that is, you must log in to a specific client to see that data.

In business terms, the **client generally represents a corporate group or a group of affiliates**. Certain configurations and master record details in the **SAP S/4HANA system** are maintained at the **client level**, meaning the specific setting is valid for the entire client.

For example:
- You can maintain a **chart of accounts** and assign it to multiple company codes.
- Activating **document splitting** in a client activates the chart of accounts for the entire client (and all company codes) by default.

### Client Settings

An administrator maintains the settings for each client (Figure 2.2). Although details are out of scope for certification, the main configurations include:

- **Client Types:**
  - Production
  - Test
  - Customizing
  - Demo
  - Training/Education
  - SAP Reference

- **Changes and Transports for Client-Specific Objects:** Controls whether an admin controls system configuration changes and packages settings for transport to other systems.

- **Cross-Client Object Changes:** Determines whether you can perform cross-client customizing from the client.

- **Client Copy and Comparison Tool Protections:** Determines whether the client can be copied or used as a reference.

### SAP S/4HANA Best Practices Packages

The implementation team generally starts in a fresh client with relevant **SAP Best Practices packages** installed. These packages contain basic configuration settings provided by country.

- Some countries have two different packages.
- You can install multiple packages as needed for your project.

> **Tip:** Installation and administration of SAP Best Practices packages are **not in scope** for the certification.

---

## 2.2.2 Company Code

A **company code** is the most fundamental organizational unit for financial accounting in **SAP S/4HANA**. It represents the **legal entity** for which a complete, self-contained set of accounts can be created.

This includes all accounts needed for posting transactions and items for legally required financial statements (e.g., **balance sheet** and **profit & loss (P&L) statement**) for local authorities.

### Company Codes in SAP S/4HANA

- Template company codes are created by the SAP Best Practices package.
- You can use Best Practices company codes directly or copy them to fit project requirements.
- Separate company codes (and packages) are created per country to meet external reporting requirements.
- A single client can support any number of company codes from multiple countries.

### Steps to Create a New Company Code

1. **Copy an existing company code.**
2. **Adjust the basic data.**
3. **Adjust the global parameters.**

---

### 1. Copy an Existing Company Code

- You enter the **reference company code (From Company Code)** and the **new company code (To Company Code)** (Figure 2.3).
- This copies:
  - Basic data
  - Global parameters
  - Customizing settings
- Optionally, also copies:
  - General ledger accounts and account determinations (Figure 2.4)
  - Assignment to the controlling area (Figure 2.5)
  - Defined local currency (Figure 2.6)

> **Note:** Directly creating a company code without copying is possible but **not recommended** due to configuration complexity and risk of errors.

---

### 2. Adjust Basic Data
